[2;36m                    [0m         [39mxmlParseAttribute2[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/home/qqor/crete/packages/python_oss_fuzz/.oss_fuzz/build/out/[0m[95mlibxml2[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m -v [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/tmp/[0m[95mtmp8cqblfw1[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m[39m -t ghcr.io/aixcc-finals/base-runner:v1.[0m[1;36m3.0[0m[39m reproduce xml[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA double-free vulnerability has been detected in the libxml2 library's XML parser. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue occurs in the `xmlParseAttribute2` function during the parsing of XML [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattributes, where a memory region at address `[0m[1;36m0x5020000008b0[0m[39m` is freed twice, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleading to a crash. This memory corruption issue was discovered through fuzzing and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhas been assigned a scariness score of [0m[1;36m42[0m[39m.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue is a classic **double-free vulnerability** detected by AddressSanitizer [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring fuzzing of the libxml2 XML parser. This type of vulnerability occurs when [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe same memory region is deallocated more than once, which can lead to memory [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorruption, crashes, and potentially exploitable security vulnerabilities.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Memory Region Affected**: The double-free occurs on a [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m-byte memory region [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstarting at address `[0m[1;36m0x5020000008b0[0m[39m`. This memory was originally allocated through [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlStrndup` via the custom memory allocator `xmlFuzzMalloc`.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Call Stack Analysis**:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The memory is first allocated in `xmlParseAttribute2` at line [0m[1;36m9009[0m[39m via [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlStrndup`[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The first free occurs at line [0m[1;36m9024[0m[39m in `xmlParseAttribute2`[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The second [0m[1;39m([0m[39merroneous[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m free occurs at line [0m[1;36m9028[0m[39m in the same function [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlParseAttribute2`[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Both frees happen within the context of `xmlParseStartTag2` calling [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlParseAttribute2`[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Execution Flow**: The vulnerability is triggered during the following [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecution sequence:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` → entry point for fuzzing[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `xmlCtxtParseDocument` → document parsing[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `xmlParseDocument` → document structure parsing[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `xmlParseElement` → element parsing[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `xmlParseElementStart` → start tag parsing[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `xmlParseStartTag2` → tag parsing with attributes[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `xmlParseAttribute2` → attribute parsing where the double-free occurs[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Deduplication Token**: The issue is identified with the token [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`__interceptor_free--xmlParseAttribute2--xmlParseStartTag2`, indicating this is a [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mknown pattern of failure.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas for Investigation:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo gain a holistic understanding of this issue, the following parts of the codebase[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould be investigated:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **`parser.c` - `xmlParseAttribute2` function** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m9009[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m9028[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: This is the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprimary location where the double-free occurs. The logic between lines [0m[1;36m9024[0m[39m and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m9028[0m[39m needs careful examination to understand why the same pointer is being freed [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtwice.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **`parser.c` - `xmlParseStartTag2` function** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m9233[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: This function calls [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlParseAttribute2` and may be involved in the attribute parsing lifecycle and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory management.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Memory allocation chain**:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `xmlstring.c` - `xmlStrndup` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m57[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Where the memory is initially[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `fuzz/fuzz.c` - `xmlFuzzMalloc` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m127[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Custom memory allocator [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mused during fuzzing[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Error handling paths**: The double-free typically occurs in error handling [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mscenarios where cleanup code may be executed multiple times or where ownership of [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory is ambiguous. The error paths in `xmlParseAttribute2` should be analyzed.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Attribute parsing logic**: The broader attribute parsing mechanism in [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`parser.c` should be reviewed to understand the expected lifecycle of attribute [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalue strings and their memory management.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Related parsing functions**: `xmlParseElementStart` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m10136[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlParseElement` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m10071[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and `xmlParseDocument` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m10902[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to understand [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe context in which attributes are parsed and how memory ownership is transferred [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor maintained across these function boundaries.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Analysis Summary[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the code snippets and the evaluation report, I have identified the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroot cause of the double-free vulnerability:[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Root Cause**: [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIn `parser.c`, the `xmlParseAttribute2` function at line [0m[1;36m9024[0m[39m incorrectly frees the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`internal_val` variable within the xml:tab validation error path. This breaks the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mestablished memory management pattern used by the xml:lang and xml:space validation[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode in the same function.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**The Issue**:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m9009[0m[39m: `internal_val` is allocated via `[0m[1;35mxmlStrndup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mval, *len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m9024[0m[39m: When xml:tab has an invalid value, `internal_val` is freed[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m9027[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m9029[0m[39m: The cleanup block checks `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39minternal_val[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and frees it again[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Since line [0m[1;36m9024[0m[39m doesn't set `internal_val = NULL` after freeing, the cleanup [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mblock at line [0m[1;36m9028[0m[39m causes a double-free[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Pattern Comparison**:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **xml:lang** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m8977[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m8986[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Allocates `internal_val`, validates, emits [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwarnings if needed, but does NOT free it explicitly[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **xml:space** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m8991[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m9004[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Allocates `internal_val`, validates, emits [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwarnings if needed, but does NOT free it explicitly  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **xml:tab** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m9008[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m9026[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Allocates `internal_val`, validates, but [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mINCORRECTLY frees it at line [0m[1;36m9024[0m[39m in the error case[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAll three handlers rely on the cleanup block at lines [0m[1;36m9027[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m9029[0m[39m to free [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`internal_val` in the success path.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Fix Implementation[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Primary Fix**:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRemove the erroneous free statement at line [0m[1;36m9024[0m[39m in `parser.c`:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: `parser.[0m[1;92mc:9020[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m9025[0m[39m`[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Current Code**:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39melse [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mxmlWarningMsg[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt, XML_WAR_TAB_VALUE,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  [0m[32m"Invalid value \"%s\" for xml:tab : \"default\", \"preserve\", [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m\"expand\", or \"skip\" expected\n"[0m[39m,[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  internal_val, NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39minternal_val[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m <-- REMOVE THIS LINE[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Fixed Code**:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39melse [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mxmlWarningMsg[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt, XML_WAR_TAB_VALUE,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  [0m[32m"Invalid value \"%s\" for xml:tab : \"default\", \"preserve\", [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m\"expand\", or \"skip\" expected\n"[0m[39m,[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  internal_val, NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Detailed Steps**:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Locate the xml:tab validation block in `xmlParseAttribute2` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m9008[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m9026[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Find the error handling path for invalid xml:tab values [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m9020[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m9025[0m[1;39m)[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Remove line [0m[1;36m9024[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39minternal_val[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Keep the warning message emission [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m9021[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m9023[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m intact[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Allow the cleanup block at lines [0m[1;36m9027[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m9029[0m[39m to handle the freeing[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why This is the Optimal Approach**:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Consistency**: The fix makes xml:tab follow the exact same memory management [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern as xml:lang and xml:space, which have been working correctly in the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcodebase.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Minimal Change**: This is a single-line removal that addresses the root cause [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout introducing new logic or changing the function's behavior.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Preserves Existing Logic**: [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The warning message is still emitted for invalid values[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The cleanup block continues to work as designed[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All validation logic remains intact[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The function's contract with its caller is unchanged[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No Memory Leaks**: The cleanup block at lines [0m[1;36m9027[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m9029[0m[39m executes before every [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msuccessful return from the function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m9033[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, ensuring `internal_val` is always [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfreed exactly once.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Safe Error Handling**: The `mem_error` and `error` labels [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m9035[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m9040[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandle the case where `val` needs to be freed, which is separate from [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`internal_val` management.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How It Addresses the Issue**:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Eliminates the Double-Free**: By removing the premature free at line [0m[1;36m9024[0m[39m, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`internal_val` is only freed once by the cleanup block at line [0m[1;36m9028[0m[39m.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Maintains Functionality**: The xml:tab validation still works correctly:[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Valid values [0m[1;39m([0m[32m"default"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"preserve"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"expand"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"skip"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m set the appropriate [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontext state[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Invalid values emit a warning and don't change the state[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Memory is properly managed in all paths[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No Side Effects**: [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The change is localized to the xml:tab error path[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other code paths or functions are affected[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The pattern is already proven by xml:lang and xml:space implementations[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effects and Mitigation**:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **[0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m Expected**: This fix simply removes a redundant and harmful free [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperation. The cleanup block was already designed to handle this responsibility.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Testing Considerations**: The fix should be verified with:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Valid xml:tab values: [0m[32m"default"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"preserve"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"expand"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"skip"[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Invalid xml:tab values: to ensure the warning is still emitted and no crash [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moccurs[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mixed xml:lang, xml:space, and xml:tab attributes in the same element[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fuzzing to ensure no new memory issues are introduced[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Similar Solutions in Codebase**:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix directly follows the pattern established by:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- xml:lang validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m8977[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m8986[0m[39m in parser.c[0m[1;39m)[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- xml:space validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m8991[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m9004[0m[39m in parser.c[0m[1;39m)[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBoth of these handlers use the same cleanup pattern without intermediate frees, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdemonstrating this is the intended design.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Relevant Code Ranges[0m                                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBased on the analysis, the following code ranges are relevant for understanding and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementing this fix:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>parser.[0m[1;92mc:8915[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m9041[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                         [2m                [0m
